<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #ffffff; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">&#167;</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;The Basket is comprised of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index, the MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index and the MSCI Emerging Markets Index. The S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index was given an initial weight of 45%, and each of the MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index and the MSCI Emerging Markets Index was given an initial weight of 27.5%</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #ffffff; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">&#167;</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;1-to-1 downside exposure to decreases in the Basket beyond a 5% decline, with up to 95% of your principal at risk</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #ffffff; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: wingdings">&#167;</font>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;All payments occur at maturity and are subject to the credit risk of Royal Bank of Canada</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 16pt"><a name="starsheader"><!--EFPlaceholder--></a>Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Linked to a Global Equity Basket, due October 28, 2016</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font color="#5b8f22">&#160;</font></div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr bgcolor="#5b8f22">
<td align="left" valign="top" width="100%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 6pt">&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 20pt">Summary</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">The Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Linked to a Global Equity Basket, due October 28, 2016 (the &#8220;notes&#8221;) are our senior unsecured debt securities. The notes are not guaranteed or insured by the Canada Deposit Insurance Corporation or the U.S. Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation or secured by collateral. <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The notes will rank equally with all of our other unsecured and unsubordinated debt. Any payments due on the notes, including any repayment of principal, will be subject to the credit risk of RBC.</font> The notes provide you a leveraged return, subject to a cap, if the Ending Value of the Market Measure, which is the Global Equity Basket described below (the &#8220;Basket&#8221;), is greater than its Starting Value. If the Ending Value is less than the Threshold Value, you will lose a portion, which could be significant, of the principal amount of your notes. Payments on the notes, including the amount you receive at maturity, will be calculated based on the $10 principal amount per unit and will depend on our credit risk and the performance of the Basket. See &#8220;Terms of the Notes&#8221; below.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">The Basket is comprised of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index, the MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index and the MSCI Emerging Markets Index (each, a &#8220;Basket Component&#8221;). On the pricing date, the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index was given an initial weight of 45%, and each of the MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index and the MSCI Emerging Markets Index was given an initial weight of 27.5%.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">The economic terms of the notes (including the Capped Value) are based on our internal funding rate, which is the rate we would pay to borrow funds through the issuance of market-linked notes and the economic terms of certain related hedging arrangements.&#160;&#160;Our internal funding rate is typically lower than the rate we would pay when we issue conventional fixed or floating rate debt securities.&#160;&#160;This difference in funding rate, as well as the underwriting discount and the hedging related charge described below, reduced the economic terms of the notes to you and the initial estimated value of the notes on the pricing date. Due to these factors, the public offering price you pay to purchase the notes is greater than the initial estimated value of the notes.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">On the cover page of this term sheet, we have provided the initial estimated value for the notes.&#160;&#160;This initial estimated value was determined based on our and our affiliates&#8217; pricing models, which take into consideration our internal funding rate and the market prices for the hedging arrangements related to the notes. For more information about the initial estimated value and the structuring of the notes, see &#8220;Structuring the Notes&#8221; on page TS-18.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 6pt">&#160;&#160;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr>
<td valign="top" width="46%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><img src="chart1.jpg" alt=""></div>
</td>
<td valign="top" width="46%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">This graph reflects the returns on the notes, based on the Participation Rate of 200%, the Threshold Value of 95% of the Starting Value, and the Capped Value of $11.73. The green line reflects the returns on the notes, while the dotted gray line reflects the returns of a direct investment in the stocks included in the Basket Components, excluding dividends.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">This graph has been prepared for purposes of illustration only.</font></div>
</div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The following table and examples are for purposes of illustration only.&#160;&#160;They are based on hypothetical values and show hypothetical returns on the notes. They illustrate the calculation of the Redemption Amount and total rate of return based on the Starting Value of 100, the Threshold Value of 95, the Participation Rate of 200%, the Capped Value of $11.73 per unit and a range of hypothetical Ending Values.<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> The actual amount you receive and the resulting total rate of return will depend on the actual Ending Value and whether you hold the notes to maturity.</font> The following examples do not take into account any tax consequences from investing in the notes.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">For recent <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">hypothetical</font> levels of the Basket, see &#8220;The Basket&#8221; section below. Each Basket Component is a price return index and as such the Ending Value will not include any income generated by dividends paid on the stocks included in any of the Basket Components, which you would otherwise be entitled to receive if you invested in those stocks directly. In addition, all payments on the notes are subject to issuer credit risk.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr>
<td colspan="2" valign="bottom" width="24%" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: black 2px solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Ending Value</font></div>
</td>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">There are important differences between the notes and a conventional debt security.&#160;&#160;An investment in the notes involves significant risks, including those listed below. You should carefully review the more detailed explanation of risks relating to the notes in the &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; sections beginning on page PS-6 of product supplement EQUITY INDICES LIRN-1, page S-1 of the MTN prospectus supplement, and page 1 of the prospectus identified above. We also urge you to consult your investment, legal, tax, accounting, and other advisors before you invest in the notes.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Payments on the notes are subject to our credit risk, and actual or perceived changes in our creditworthiness are expected to affect the value of the notes.&#160;&#160;If we become insolvent or are unable to pay our obligations, you may lose your entire investment.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 17.45pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Your investment return, if any, is limited to the return represented by the Capped Value and may be less than a comparable investment directly in the stocks included in the Basket Components.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 17.45pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The initial estimated value of the notes is an estimate only, determined as of a particular point in time by reference to our and our affiliates&#8217; pricing models. These pricing models consider certain assumptions and variables, including our credit spreads, our internal funding rate on the pricing date, mid-market terms on hedging transactions, expectations on interest rates and volatility, price-sensitivity analysis, and the expected term of the notes. These pricing models rely in part on certain forecasts about future events, which may prove to be incorrect.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 17.45pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The public offering price you pay for the notes exceeds the initial estimated value. If you attempt to sell the notes prior to maturity, their market value may be lower than the price you paid for them and lower than the initial estimated value. This is due to, among other things, changes in the level of the Basket, our internal funding rate, and the inclusion in the public offering price of the underwriting discount and the hedging related charge, all as further described in &#8220;Structuring the Notes&#8221; on page TS-18. These factors, together with various credit, market and economic factors over the term of the notes, are expected to reduce the price at which you may be able to sell the notes in any secondary market and will affect the value of the notes in complex and unpredictable ways.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The initial estimated value does not represent a minimum or maximum price at which we, MLPF&amp;S or any of our affiliates would be willing to purchase your notes in any secondary market (if any exists) at any time. The value of your notes at any time after issuance will vary based on many factors that cannot be predicted with accuracy, including the performance of the Basket, our creditworthiness and changes in market conditions.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Linked to a Global Equity Basket, due October 28, 2016</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font color="#5b8f22">&#160;</font></div>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">

<td align="left" valign="top" width="92%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 6pt">&#160;&#160;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 20pt">Other Terms of the Notes</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Market Measure Business Day</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The following definition shall supersede and replace the definition of a &#8220;Market Measure Business Day&#8221; set forth in product supplement EQUITY INDICES LIRN-1 dated December 23, 2013.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">A &#8220;Market Measure Business Day&#8221; means a day on which:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">(A) each of the New York Stock Exchange and NASDAQ Stock Market, Inc. (as to the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index), the London Stock Exchange, Frankfurt Stock Exchange, Paris Bourse, Tokyo Stock Exchange (as to the MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index), and the London Stock Exchange, Hong Kong Stock Exchange, S&#227;o Paulo Stock Exchange and Korea Stock Exchange (as to the MSCI Emerging Markets Index) (or any successor to the foregoing exchanges) are open for trading; and</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">(B) the Basket Components or any successors thereto are calculated and published.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<td align="left" valign="top" width="92%" style="BORDER-TOP: #5b8f22 0.5pt solid">

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 20pt"><a name="underlying_description"><!--EFPlaceholder--></a>The Basket</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The Basket is designed to allow investors to participate in the percentage changes in the levels of the Basket Components from the Starting Value to the Ending Value of the Basket. The Basket Components are described in the section &#8220;The Basket Components&#8221; below. Each Basket Component will be assigned an initial weight on the pricing date, as set forth in the table below.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">For more information on the calculation of the value of the Basket, please see the section entitled &#8220;Description of LIRNs&#8212;Basket Market Measures&#8221; beginning on page PS-19 of product supplement EQUITY INDICES LIRN-1.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">(1)</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">

<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">(2)</font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Each Component Ratio equals the Initial Component Weight of the relevant Basket Component (as a percentage) multiplied by 100, and then divided by the closing level of that Basket Component on the pricing date and rounded to eight decimal places.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The calculation agent will calculate the value of the Basket by summing the products of the closing level for each Basket Component on each calculation day during the Maturity Valuation Period and the Component Ratio applicable to such Basket Component. If a Market Disruption Event occurs as to any Basket Component on any scheduled calculation day, the closing level of that Basket Component will be determined as more fully described in the section entitled &#8220;Description of LIRNs&#8212;Basket Market Measures&#8212;Ending Value of the Basket&#8221; beginning on page PS-20 of product supplement EQUITY INDICES LIRN-1.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 16pt">Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Linked to a Global Equity Basket, due October 28, 2016</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 16pt">Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Linked to a Global Equity Basket, due October 28, 2016</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font color="#5b8f22">&#160;</font></div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr bgcolor="#5b8f22">
<td align="left" valign="top" width="92%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 6pt">&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>&#160;</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 20pt">The Basket Components</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">All disclosures contained in this term sheet regarding the Basket Components, including, without limitation, their make up, method of calculation, and changes in their components, have been derived from publicly available sources. The information reflects the policies of, and is subject to change by, the applicable index sponsor. The index sponsors have no obligation to continue to publish, and may discontinue publication of, any Basket Component. The consequences of an index sponsor discontinuing publication of a Basket Component are discussed in the section entitled &#8220;Description of LIRNs&#8212;Discontinuance of an Index&#8221; beginning on page PS-18 of product supplement EQUITY INDICES LIRN-1.&#160;&#160;None of us, the calculation agent, or MLPF&amp;S accepts any responsibility for the calculation, maintenance or publication of any Basket Component or any successor index.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is intended to provide an indication of the pattern of common stock price movement. The calculation of the level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is based on the relative value of the aggregate market value of the common stocks of 500 companies as of a particular time compared to the aggregate average market value of the common stocks of 500 similar companies during the base period of the years 1941 through 1943.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">S&amp;P Dow Jones Indices LLC (&#8220;S&amp;P&#8221; or the &#8220;index sponsor&#8221;) chooses companies for inclusion in the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index with the aim of achieving a distribution by broad industry groupings that approximates the distribution of these groupings in the common stock population of its Stock Guide Database of over 10,000 companies, which S&amp;P uses as an assumed model for the composition of the total market. Relevant criteria employed by S&amp;P include the viability of the particular company, the extent to which that company represents the industry group to which it is assigned, the extent to which the market price of that company&#8217;s common stock generally is responsive to changes in the affairs of the respective industry and the market value and trading activity of the common stock of that company. Ten main groups of companies constitute the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, with the approximate percentage of the market capitalization of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index included in each group as of September 30<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">th</font>, 2014 indicated in parentheses: Consumer Discretionary (11.7%); Consumer Staples (9.5%); Energy (9.7%); Financials (16.3%); Health Care (13.9%); Industrials (10.3%); Information Technology (19.7%); Materials (3.5%); Telecommunication Services (2.4%); and Utilities (3.0%). The S&amp;P may from time to time, in its sole discretion, add companies to, or delete companies from, the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index to achieve the objectives stated above.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">S&amp;P calculates the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index by reference to the prices of the constituent stocks of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index without taking account of the value of dividends paid on those stocks. As a result, the return on the notes will not reflect the return you would realize if you actually owned the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index constituent stocks and received the dividends paid on those stocks.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Computation of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">While S&amp;P currently employs the following methodology to calculate the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, no assurance can be given that S&amp;P will not modify or change this methodology in a manner that may affect the Redemption Amount.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Historically, the market value of any component stock of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index was calculated as the product of the market price per share and the number of then outstanding shares of such component stock. In March 2005, S&amp;P began shifting the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index halfway from a market capitalization weighted formula to a float-adjusted formula, before moving the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index to full float adjustment on September 16, 2005. S&amp;P&#8217;s criteria for selecting stocks for the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index did not change with the shift to float adjustment. However, the adjustment affects each company&#8217;s weight in the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Under float adjustment, the share counts used in calculating the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index reflect only those shares that are available to investors, not all of a company&#8217;s outstanding shares.&#160;&#160;Float adjustment excludes shares that are closely held by control groups, other publicly traded companies or government agencies.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">In September 2012, all shareholdings representing more than 5% of a stock&#8217;s outstanding shares, other than holdings by &#8220;block owners,&#8221; were removed from the float for purposes of calculating the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index.&#160;&#160;Generally, these &#8220;control holders&#8221; will include officers and directors, private equity, venture capital and special equity firms, other publicly traded companies that hold shares for control, strategic partners, holders of restricted shares, ESOPs, employee and family trusts, foundations associated with the company, holders of unlisted share classes of stock, government entities at all levels (other than government retirement/pension funds) and any individual person who controls a 5% or greater stake in a company as reported in regulatory filings.&#160;&#160;However, holdings by block owners, such as depositary banks, pension funds, mutual funds and ETF providers, 401(k) plans of the company, government retirement/pension funds, investment funds of insurance companies, asset managers and investment funds, independent foundations and savings and investment plans, will ordinarily be considered part of the float.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Treasury stock, stock options, restricted shares, equity participation units, warrants, preferred stock, convertible stock, and rights are not part of the float. Shares held in a trust to allow investors in countries outside the country of domicile, such as depositary shares and Canadian exchangeable shares are normally part of the float unless those shares form a control block.&#160;&#160;If a company has multiple classes of stock outstanding, shares in an unlisted or non-traded class are treated as a control block.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">For each stock, an investable weight factor (&#8220;IWF&#8221;) is calculated by dividing the available float shares by the total shares outstanding.&#160;&#160;As of September 21, 2012, available float shares are defined as the total shares outstanding less shares held by control holders.&#160;&#160;This calculation is subject to a 5% minimum threshold for control blocks.&#160;&#160;For example, if a company&#8217;s officers and directors hold 3% of the company&#8217;s shares, and no other control group holds 5% of the company&#8217;s shares, S&amp;P would assign that company an IWF of 1.00, as no control group meets the 5% threshold.&#160;&#160;However, if a company&#8217;s officers and directors hold 3% of the company&#8217;s shares and another control group holds 20% of the company&#8217;s shares, S&amp;P would assign an IWF of 0.77, reflecting the fact that 23% of the company&#8217;s outstanding shares are considered to be held for control.&#160;&#160;For companies with multiple classes of stock, S&amp;P calculates the weighted average IWF for each stock using the proportion of the total company market capitalization of each share class as weights.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="92%" style="BORDER-TOP: #5b8f22 0.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><a name="starsfooter"><!--efplaceholder--></a>Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div id="PGBRK" style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt">
<div id="PN" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; WIDTH: 100%">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; WIDTH: 100%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">TS-10</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; WIDTH: 100%">
<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 16pt">Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b8f22; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Linked to a Global Equity Basket, due October 28, 2016</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font color="#5b8f22">&#160;</font></div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr bgcolor="#5b8f22">
<td align="left" valign="top" width="92%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 6pt">&#160;&#160;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is calculated using a base-weighted aggregate methodology. The level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index reflects the total market value of all 500 component stocks relative to the base period of the years 1941 through 1943. An indexed number is used to represent the results of this calculation in order to make the level easier to work with and track over time. The actual total market value of the component stocks during the base period of the years 1941 through 1943 has been set to an indexed level of 10. This is often indicated by the notation 1941- 43 = 10. In practice, the daily calculation of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is computed by dividing the total market value of the component stocks by the &#8220;index divisor.&#8221; By itself, the index divisor is an arbitrary number. However, in the context of the calculation of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, it serves as a link to the original base period level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index. The index divisor keeps the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index comparable over time and is the manipulation point for all adjustments to the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, which is index maintenance.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Index Maintenance</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Index maintenance includes monitoring and completing the adjustments for company additions and deletions, share changes, stock splits, stock dividends, and stock price adjustments due to company restructuring or spinoffs. Some corporate actions, such as stock splits and stock dividends, require changes in the common shares outstanding and the stock prices of the companies in the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, and do not require index divisor adjustments.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">To prevent the level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index from changing due to corporate actions, corporate actions which affect the total market value of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index require an index divisor adjustment. By adjusting the index divisor for the change in market value, the level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index remains constant and does not reflect the corporate actions of individual companies in the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index. Index divisor adjustments are made after the close of trading and after the calculation of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index closing level.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Changes in a company&#8217;s shares outstanding of 5.00% or more due to mergers, acquisitions, public offerings, tender offers, Dutch auctions, or exchange offers are made as soon as reasonably possible. All other changes of 5.00% or more (due to, for example, company stock repurchases, private placements, redemptions, exercise of options, warrants, conversion of preferred stock, notes, debt, equity participation units, at-the-market offerings, or other recapitalizations) are made weekly and are announced on Wednesdays for implementation after the close of trading on the following Wednesday. Changes of less than 5.00% due to a company's acquisition of another company in the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index are made as soon as reasonably possible. All other changes of less than 5.00% are accumulated and made quarterly on the third Friday of March, June, September, and December, and are usually announced two to five days prior.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Changes in IWFs of more than five percentage points caused by corporate actions (such as merger and acquisition activity, restructurings, or spinoffs) will be made as soon as reasonably possible. Other changes in IWFs will be made annually when IWFs are reviewed.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The following graph shows the historical performance of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index in the period from January 2008 through September 2014. We obtained this historical data from Bloomberg L.P.&#160;&#160;We have not independently verified the accuracy or completeness of the information obtained from Bloomberg L.P. On the pricing date, the closing level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index was 1,994.65.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Historical Performance of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><img src="chart3.jpg" alt=""></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">This historical data on the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index is not necessarily indicative of the future performance of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index or what the value of the notes may be. Any historical upward or downward trend in the level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index during any period set forth above is not an indication that the level of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index is more or less likely to increase or decrease at any time over the term of the notes.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Before investing in the notes, you should consult publicly available sources for the levels and trading pattern of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174; </font>Index.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The MSCI EAFE</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#174;</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> Index</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">MSCI Inc. (&#8220;MSCI&#8221;) is the index sponsor of the MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index. The MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is intended to measure equity market performance in developed market countries, excluding the U.S. and Canada. The MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is a free float-adjusted market capitalization equity index with a base date of December 31, 1969 and an initial value of 100.00. The MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is calculated daily in U.S. dollars and published in real time every 60 seconds during market trading hours. The MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index currently consists of companies from the following 21 developed countries: Australia, Austria, Belgium, Denmark, Finland, France, Germany, Hong Kong, Ireland, Israel, Italy, Japan, the Netherlands, New Zealand, Norway, Portugal, Singapore, Spain, Sweden, Switzerland, and the United Kingdom. As of September 30, 2014, the five largest country weights were Britain (21.3%), Japan (21.0%), France (9.9%), Switzerland (9.2%), and Germany (8.8%), and the five largest sector weights were Financials (25.7%), Industrials&#160;&#160;(12.5%), Consumer Discretionary (11.6%), Healthcare (11.2%), and Consumer Staples (10.9%).</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The MSCI EAFE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index is part of the MSCI Regional Equity Indices series and is an MSCI Global Investable Market Index, which is a family within the MSCI International Equity Indices.</font></div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The MSCI Emerging Markets Index</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">MSCI is the index sponsor of the MSCI Emerging Markets Index. The MSCI Emerging Markets Index is intended to measure equity market performance in the global emerging markets. The MSCI Emerging Markets Index is a free float-adjusted market capitalization index with a base date of December 31, 1987 and an initial value of 100.00. The MSCI Emerging Markets Index is calculated daily in U.S. dollars and published in real time every 60 seconds during market trading hours. The MSCI Emerging Markets Index currently consists of the following 24 emerging market country indices: Brazil, Chile, China, Colombia, Czech Republic, Egypt, Greece, Hungary, India, Indonesia, Korea, Malaysia, Mexico, Peru, Philippines, Poland, Qatar, Russia, South Africa, South Korea, Taiwan, Thailand, Turkey, and the United Arab Emirates. As of September 30, 2014, the five largest country weights were China (19.2%), South Korea (15.0%), Taiwan (12.0%), Brazil (10.3%), and South Africa (7.4%), and the five largest sector weights were Financials (27.5%), Information Technology (16.7%), Energy (10.2%), Consumer Discretionary (9.0%), and Consumer Staples (8.3%).</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The MSCI Emerging Markets Index is part of the MSCI Regional Equity Indices series and is an MSCI Global Investable Market Index, which is a family within the MSCI International Equity Indices.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">General - MSCI Indices</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">MSCI provides global equity indices intended to measure equity performance in international markets and the MSCI International Equity Indices are designed to serve as global equity performance benchmarks. In constructing these indices, MSCI applies its index construction and maintenance methodology across developed, emerging, and frontier markets.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">MSCI enhanced the methodology used in its MSCI International Equity Indices. The MSCI Standard and MSCI Small Cap Indices, along with the other MSCI equity indices based on them, transitioned to the global investable market indices methodology described below. The transition was completed at the end of May 2008. The Enhanced MSCI Standard Indices are composed of the MSCI Large Cap and Mid Cap Indices. The MSCI Global Small Cap Index transitioned to the MSCI Small Cap Index resulting from the Global Investable Market Indices methodology and contains no overlap with constituents of the transitioned MSCI Standard Indices. Together, the relevant MSCI Large Cap, Mid Cap, and Small Cap Indices will make up the MSCI investable market index for each country, composite, sector, and style index that MSCI offers.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Constructing the MSCI Global Investable Market Indices.</font>&#160;&#160;MSCI undertakes an index construction process, which involves:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">defining the equity universe;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">determining the market investable equity universe for each market;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">determining market capitalization size segments for each market;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">applying index continuity rules for the MSCI Standard Index;</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">creating style segments within each size segment within each market; and</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">classifying securities under the Global Industry Classification Standard (the &#8220;GICS&#8221;).</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Defining the Equity Universe.</font>&#160;&#160;The equity universe is defined by:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Identifying Eligible Equity Securities: the equity universe initially looks at securities listed in any of the countries in the MSCI Global Index Series, which will be classified as either Developed Markets (&#8220;DM&#8221;) or Emerging Markets (&#8220;EM&#8221;). All listed equity securities, or listed securities that exhibit characteristics of equity securities, except mutual funds, ETFs, equity derivatives, limited partnerships, and most investment trusts, are eligible for inclusion in the equity universe. Real Estate Investment Trusts (&#8220;REITs&#8221;) in some countries and certain income trusts in Canada are also eligible for inclusion.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Classifying Eligible Securities into the Appropriate Country: each company and its securities (i.e., share classes) are classified in only one country.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Determining the Market Investable Equity Universes.&#160;&#160;</font>A market investable equity universe for a market is derived by applying investability screens to individual companies and securities in the equity universe that are classified in that market. A market is equivalent to a single country, except in DM Europe, where all DM countries in Europe are aggregated into a single market for index construction purposes. Subsequently, individual DM Europe country indices within the MSCI Europe Index are derived from the constituents of the MSCI Europe Index under the global investable market indices methodology.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">The investability screens used to determine the investable equity universe in each market are as follows:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Equity Universe Minimum Size Requirement: this investability screen is applied at the company level. In order to be included in a market investable equity universe, a company must have the required minimum full market capitalization.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">Equity Universe Minimum Free Float-Adjusted Market Capitalization Requirement: this investability screen is applied at the individual security level. To be eligible for inclusion in a market investable equity universe, a security must have a free float-adjusted market capitalization equal to or higher than 50% of the equity universe minimum size requirement.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 7pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Symbol, serif">&#183;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 9pt">DM and EM Minimum Liquidity Requirement: this investability screen is applied at the individual security level. To be eligible for inclusion in a market investable equity universe, a security must have adequate liquidity. The twelve-month and three-month Annual Traded Value Ratio (&#8220;ATVR&#8221;), a measure that screens out extreme daily trading volumes and takes into account the free float-adjusted market capitalization size of securities, together with the three-month frequency of trading are used to measure liquidity. In the calculation of the ATVR, the trading volumes in depository receipts associated with that security, such as ADRs or GDRs, are also considered. A minimum liquidity level of 20% of three- and twelve-month ATVR and 90% of three-month frequency of trading over the last four consecutive quarters are required for inclusion of a security in a market investable equity universe of a DM, and a minimum liquidity level of 15% of three- and twelve-month ATVR and 80% of three-month frequency of trading over the last four consecutive quarters are required for inclusion of a security in a market investable equity universe of an EM.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="92%" style="BORDER-TOP: #5b8f22 0.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #5b862b; FONT-SIZE: 9pt"><a name="starsfooter"><!--efplaceholder--></a>Capped Leveraged Index Return Notes<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
